[世界人权日，证福建政法系统教育整顿造假联署达745人](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/745.html)
------

<div>
<span><a name='more'></a></span><p><br /></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">第一批政法教育整顿，截至</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">8</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">18</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，福建省教育整顿办已办结群众举报线索</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">9137</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">件，查结率达</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">94.02%</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">，此次整顿结果得到全国教育整顿办和中央第八督导组的肯定，群众好评率达</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">99.08%</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span></b><b><span style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">第二批政法教育整顿，截至</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">10</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月底</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">,</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">中央信访联席办交办我省</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">10691</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">件重复信访事项</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">,</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">已经化解</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">9848</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">件</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">,</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">占</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">92.1%</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; text-indent: 21.1pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">为了证实上述统计数据公开造假瞒报，福建众冤民识破政法腐败的毒瘤，将每个未查实名数据来揭开上述荒唐伪据，每次教育整顿督导组、巡视组都见不上，省政府、公安厅对他们层层保护，与访民隔绝，从何谈上查结率达</span><span lang="EN-US">94.02%</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; text-indent: 21.1pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">纵观如下未查实名众冤触目惊心，令人发指，政法腐败，巡视造假，打压维权，有法不依，有案不立，有腐不惩，有黑不除，充当保护，权钱交易，侵权渎职，徇私枉法，执法犯法，是福建执政执法的严重腐败，自受害例举名单与统计数据对照恰恰相反，众冤强烈呼吁对该伪造数据确定质疑，追责散布该虚假信息的意图罪责，背弃初心使命担当，侵害维权切身利益，践踏法律尊严，歪曲事实真相，在拆迁和政法被害的众冤，维权数年不等，甚至受害被打压成罪犯软拘囚禁，变相制造冤假错案，打击报复维权人，福建莆田欧金中就是其中最典型一例被活活逼死轰动全国，福建让谁好评？只是彰显腐败黄婆卖瓜自卖自夸，害了百姓民不聊生。</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; text-indent: 21.1pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">针对福建政法整顿屡次造假数据证明，福建众多冤民都没有解决，瞒报查结率达</span><span lang="EN-US">94.02%</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">不作为乱作为的严重腐败，实名众冤呐喊中央各上级领导高度重视和关注，对福建典型腐败造假专案督查督办，体现党的英明政策！</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><b><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">以下未查实名众冤呈上明鉴！</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; text-align: left; text-indent: 21.0pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、黄思静，女，厦门市思明区</span> <span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">，电话</span><span lang="EN-US">15359838218</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、方国建，男，福州市闽侯县青口镇，电话</span><span lang="EN-US">13110530880</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、施惠卿，女，福州市晋安区，电话</span><span lang="EN-US">18759170451</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、范巧珠，女，福建省闽清县梅城镇，电话</span><span lang="EN-US">15060198195</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、杜其雄，男，福建省永泰县霞拔乡</span><span lang="EN-US">15880155591</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">，杜其钟，男，福建永泰县霞拔乡霞拔村坑里</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">电话</span><span lang="EN-US">18659172295</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。杜其强被肇事司机重复碾压致死同个案件。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 18.0pt; margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd; text-align: left; vertical-align: baseline;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、郑昌辉，男，福州台江区清辉文化工艺厂，电话</span><span lang="EN-US">13906934274</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;
